An episode triggered by a 10% off dining coupon for staying guests.
Because we were hungry, our family of three completed the check-in procedures, put down our luggage in the room, and went to the Chinese restaurant on the second floor. My husband wanted a private room, but the waiter said that we can’t do a private room without a reservation in advance. OK, let’s eat in the lobby, and then The waiter said that their restaurant has a 15% service charge, which we accept. As a result, after ordering the meal, the waiter disappeared~ The men and women who served the food were also different. He asked for hot water with the boy who served the food. He brought a pot, put it down, and left. Wait for my daughter to think about it+ Bottle of drink, waited for a long time, only to see a waiter wearing clothes passing by, hurriedly called to stop, and then ordered~ After eating like this, I went back to the room, because I had to go to the car to pick up something for the child, I found the room card origami There is also a 10% discount coupon (as shown in the picture below), I thought I didn't use the coupon, the hotel can always give me a breakfast coupon, right? (Dining costs 1312 yuan) By the way, I went to the front desk to ask. The handsome guy at the front desk said that the coupon was used in the Chinese restaurant and asked me to communicate with the Chinese restaurant. I went to the Chinese restaurant on the second floor and explained to the cashier. Asked for a breakfast coupon, she said she would call to ask for instructions, but the phone rang a girl dressed as a waiter and asked me to tell her. I explained how the coupon was useless, and the beauty "responded" very quickly. She came up and said that I had paid for the meal and could not get a refund; I said that my discount coupon was useless after all, and I could give me a breakfast coupon ? In the end, she told me that the 10% discount on this coupon was a previous event, and the event had expired... This is not a big deal, and it is extremely insulting! After the event is over, give me a coupon for the one who just checked in? !
10,000 words omitted here......
As far as this matter is concerned, although the final processing result is considered satisfactory, the process I have experienced is quite tortuous for me. Whether it is the front desk of the hotel or the restaurant, the overall service is not satisfactory.

msg:酒店臨街顯得比較拘謹，外觀似無驚人之處，大堂顯得比較大氣上檔次，房間挺寬敞，設施和裝潢佈置挺有品位而時尚，服務員的意識比較強和有素質，索要額外的礦泉水也不吝嗇，還送了果盤。無線網絡信號強，房間光源功能區分細緻，書桌有個枱燈挺實用，床頭有電源插座，手機充電應用挺方便；洗手間乾濕分開，有淋浴軟管花灑，淋浴熱水量大感覺爽；洗臉池斜坡因有倒鈎設定不易水漫金山。房門有防盜鎖鏈扣使客人有安全感。
酒店設有自助餐還挺紅火；餐廳環境看着挺大氣，中西自助早餐品種很多，豐富可口。有地下負二層停車場，安全便捷，前台報車牌號掃描抬桿出場。
    某些細節還是有改進的空間，比如依然擺脱不了把空調冷暖調控功能任意簡化為風調這個三北地區酒店漠視客人消費體驗需求通病的怪圈，五百多的房價還得不到應有舒適的消費體驗；説是把我們安排到背面朝向居民樓安靜的房間，實側面對快速路的噪音幹擾，關窗房間又沉悶；枕頭太軟和，感覺不踏實。

posted:Posted February 26, 2022
msg:第一酒店的房間還挺大的，裏面佈置的也比較温馨。我們是春節的時候過去的人比較少，服務比較熱情，主動幫我們家增加了一個早餐，免費的。東北的冬天外面巨冷，房間裏面很熱的。非常的舒服。出去玩的話這個地方也挺好的，就是比較容易的就出城了，不用在城市裡麪繞，因為冰雪項目基本上都在城外。還有，免費的迎賓水果。是一個好的賓館。
最後如果可以改進的地方，那就是早餐的種類建議能更多一點。時間上能夠開到10:00，現在9:30的話，對於玩的人可能還是偏早的。
